<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Proposed_services">Proposed services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Proposed services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="CrossCountry_Trains_Consultation_2018">CrossCountry Trains Consultation 2018</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: CrossCountry Trains Consultation 2018">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The Department for Transport's 2018 consultation on the future of the CrossCountry franchise, which was due for renewal in 2019 but was later cancelled in September 2018<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> but cited Liverpool as a potential new destination for CrossCountry train service. If adopted this may restore some of the services lost in 2003. The Consultation closed in August 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Despite the cancellation of the competition, the consultation responses will be used to help develop options for the future of the franchise so Liverpool may be considered as a potential destination in the future.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Long_Term_Rail_Strategy_Proposals">Long Term Rail Strategy Proposals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Long Term Rail Strategy Proposals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In a long term rail strategy by Merseytravel, new direct services to Cardiff, Bristol, Leicester, Derby, Glasgow Central and Edinburgh Waverley have been proposed.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Virgin_Open_Access_Proposal">Virgin Open Access Proposal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Virgin Open Access Proposal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In June 2019, Virgin lodged an application for an open access service from <a href="/wiki/London_Euston_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="London Euston railway station">London Euston</a> to Liverpool Lime Street calling at <a href="/wiki/Nuneaton_railway_station" title="Nuneaton railway station">Nuneaton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tamworth_railway_station" title="Tamworth railway station">Tamworth</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lichfield_Trent_Valley_railway_station" title="Lichfield Trent Valley railway station">Lichfield Trent Valley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_South_Parkway_railway_station" title="Liverpool South Parkway railway station">Liverpool South Parkway</a> and Liverpool Lime Street to rival the future <a href="/wiki/West_Coast_Partnership" class="mw-redirect" title="West Coast Partnership">West Coast Partnership</a> franchisee from May 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="West_Coast_Partnership">West Coast Partnership</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: West Coast Partnership">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In August 2019, it was announced that <a href="/wiki/FirstGroup" title="FirstGroup">FirstGroup</a> <a href="/wiki/Trenitalia" title="Trenitalia">Trenitalia</a> would operate the <a href="/wiki/West_Coast_Partnership" class="mw-redirect" title="West Coast Partnership">West Coast Partnership</a> franchise from December 2019. As part of the award, the new operator will look at providing up to two trains per hour between Liverpool Lime Street and <a href="/wiki/London_Euston_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="London Euston railway station">London Euston</a> from December 2022, subject to approval by the <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Rail_and_Road" title="Office of Rail and Road">Office of Rail and Road</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Future_Northern_and_TransPennine_Franchises">Future Northern and TransPennine Franchises</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Future Northern and TransPennine Franchises">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In November 2018, it was revealed by Transport for the North several options for the future Northern and TransPennine franchise. Some options for Liverpool include extension of Liverpool to Crewe services towards Stoke-on-Trent and Alsager, increasing Liverpool to Blackpool North services and a new Liverpool to Leicester service via Crewe, Stoke-on-Trent, Uttoxeter and Derby. The Leicester service could be operated by either TransPennine Express or the future East Midlands Franchise.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="TransPennine_Franchise_Agreement">TransPennine Franchise Agreement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: TransPennine Franchise Agreement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As part of the TransPennine Express (TPE) franchise agreement (awarded to <a href="/wiki/TransPennine_Express" title="TransPennine Express">FirstGroup</a> which started services in April 2016), there will be three new direct services per day to Glasgow Central via Preston along the West Coast main line.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>  The current hourly TPE Newcastle route will also be extended via <a href="/wiki/Morpeth_railway_station" title="Morpeth railway station">Morpeth</a> to <a href="/wiki/Edinburgh_Waverley" class="mw-redirect" title="Edinburgh Waverley">Edinburgh Waverley</a>.
</p><p>In 2005 <a href="/wiki/Renaissance_Trains" title="Renaissance Trains">Renaissance Trains</a> proposed a <a href="/wiki/Glasgow_Trains" title="Glasgow Trains">twice-daily service</a> from Lime Street to <a href="/wiki/Glasgow_Central_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Glasgow Central railway station">Glasgow Central</a>, with weekend trains running instead from <a href="/wiki/Blackpool_North_railway_station" title="Blackpool North railway station">Blackpool</a> to Glasgow.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> The proposal did not get enough investment backing, but was revived in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Chester.2C_Wales_and_Shrewsbury_via_the_Halton_Curve"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Chester,_Wales_and_Shrewsbury_via_the_Halton_Curve">Chester, Wales and Shrewsbury via the Halton Curve</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Chester, Wales and Shrewsbury via the Halton Curve">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The completion of the upgrade of the <a href="/wiki/Halton_Curve" title="Halton Curve">Halton Curve</a> in 2018 provides a second rail route between Liverpool and Chester, and permits the introduction of new direct services from Liverpool to Wrexham, Llandudno and other parts of <a href="/wiki/North_Wales" title="North Wales">North Wales</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-NewWelshFranchise_92-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NewWelshFranchise-92">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> 
As part of the new Wales &amp; Borders franchise services to Chester were  introduced in May 2019 with future services to Llandudno and Shrewsbury every hour and services to Cardiff every two hours planned.<sup id="cite_ref-NewWelshFranchise_92-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NewWelshFranchise-92">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="London_Euston">London Euston</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: London Euston">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>It was also proposed by 2016 that London Midland will also operate an hourly service to London Euston (as an extension of its existing Trent Valley semi-fast service).<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="margin-left:0.1em; white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers"><span title="The text near this tag is dated. (August 2016)">needs update</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>. From May 2019, its successor <a href="/wiki/London_Northwestern_Railway" class="mw-redirect" title="London Northwestern Railway">London Northwestern Railway</a> operates a London to Liverpool service via Birmingham New Street.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Northern_Franchise_Agreement">Northern Franchise Agreement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Northern Franchise Agreement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As part of the Northern franchise agreement (awarded to <a href="/wiki/Northern_(train_operating_company)" title="Northern (train operating company)">Arriva</a>, which started in April 2016), from December 2019 there will be a new "Northern Connect" service to Leeds via Manchester Victoria and Bradford Interchange (replacing the current all-stations local service to Victoria).<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> This is the first time there is a direct service through to Rochdale, Halifax and Bradford Interchange since the timetable change on 10 December 2006 when Northern terminated all services at Manchester Victoria.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Withdrawn_services">Withdrawn services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Withdrawn services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Certain direct trains to and from Liverpool Lime Street station have been withdrawn since 2000. These include the following services:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wales_%26_West" title="Wales &amp; West">Wales &amp; West</a> services to <a href="/wiki/Cardiff_Central_railway_station" title="Cardiff Central railway station">Cardiff</a> and <a href="/wiki/Milford_Haven_railway_station" title="Milford Haven railway station">Milford Haven</a> via the <a href="/wiki/Welsh_Marches" title="Welsh Marches">Welsh Marches</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Virgin_CrossCountry" title="Virgin CrossCountry">Virgin CrossCountry</a> services to <a href="/wiki/Edinburgh_Waverley_railway_station" title="Edinburgh Waverley railway station">Edinburgh</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poole_railway_station" title="Poole railway station">Poole</a>, <a href="/wiki/Weymouth_railway_station" title="Weymouth railway station">Weymouth</a>, <a href="/wiki/London_Paddington_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="London Paddington railway station">London Paddington</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth_Harbour_railway_station" title="Portsmouth Harbour railway station">Portsmouth</a>, <a href="/wiki/Plymouth_railway_station" title="Plymouth railway station">Plymouth</a> and <a href="/wiki/Brighton_railway_station" title="Brighton railway station">Brighton</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/First_North_Western" title="First North Western">First North Western</a> services to <a href="/wiki/Chester_railway_station" title="Chester railway station">Chester</a> via <a href="/wiki/Warrington_Bank_Quay_railway_station" title="Warrington Bank Quay railway station">Warrington Bank Quay</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Central_Trains" title="Central Trains">Central Trains</a> services to <a href="/wiki/Cambridge_railway_station" title="Cambridge railway station">Cambridge</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stansted_Airport_railway_station" title="Stansted Airport railway station">Stansted Airport</a>.</li></ul>
<p>In addition, former <a href="/wiki/British_Rail" title="British Rail">British Rail</a> services to Scotland, Wrexham and other parts of North Wales, <a href="/wiki/Bradford_Interchange_railway_station" class="mw-redirect" title="Bradford Interchange railway station">Bradford Interchange</a>, Harwich and Leicester no longer operate.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Underground_station">Underground station</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Underground station">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Merseyrail_Class_507,_507003,_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_(geograph_4500645).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg/220px-Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg/330px-Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg/440px-Merseyrail_Class_507%2C_507003%2C_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_%28geograph_4500645%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="683" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Merseyrail_Class_507,_507003,_Liverpool_Lime_Street_underground_station_(geograph_4500645).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The refurbished Wirral Line platform, at Lime Street underground station in 2015, with a Merseyrail <a href="/wiki/British_Rail_Class_507" title="British Rail Class 507">Class 507</a> service</div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_underground_stations_of_the_Merseyrail_network" title="List of underground stations of the Merseyrail network">List of underground stations of the Merseyrail network</a></div>
<p>The underground station consists of a single platform (sometimes referred to as Platform L<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (August 2019)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>),  alongside the 1970s <i>Liverpool Loop tunnel</i> and a ticket hall above. The station, opened in 1977, is connected to the mainline station by means of a pedestrian subway and escalators, accessed via a long passageway which crosses beneath Lime Street itself, and by a lift from the main concourse.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2013_refurbishment">2013 refurbishment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: 2013 refurbishment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Network_Rail" title="Network Rail">Network Rail</a> announced in early 2013 that Lime Street was to be the third station to be refurbished as part of the £40&#160;million investment which would see all Merseyrail underground stations excluding <a href="/wiki/Conway_Park_railway_station" title="Conway Park railway station">Conway Park</a> refurbished. This included the refurbishment of the platform and the booking hall. The station refurbishment work took place between April and August 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Subway_refurbishment">Subway refurbishment</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Subway refurbishment">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The subway linking the underground station to the mainline station was refurbished in June 2014. The subway was fitted out with new tiles, lighting, flooring and automatic doors to some of the entrances.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Recent_history">Recent history</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Recent history">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The underground station had WiFi installed in January 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2016, it was announced that the Wirral Line loop would be having its track renewed. The underground station was closed between 3 January 2017 and 18 June 2017 whilst the works took place.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Services_2">Services</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Liverpool_Lime_Street_railway_station&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Services">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Services operate on a 5-minute frequency Monday-Saturday, and between 5- and 10-minute frequency on Sundays in the winter. All trains travel through to <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Central_railway_station" title="Liverpool Central railway station">Liverpool Central</a> and <a href="/wiki/Birkenhead" title="Birkenhead">Birkenhead</a> of which:
</p>
<ul><li>4 trains per hour continue to New Brighton</li>
<li>4 trains per hour continue to West Kirby</li>
<li>4 trains per hour continue to Chester</li>
<li>2 trains per hour continue to Ellesmere Port</li></ul>
<p>To reach destinations on the <a href="/wiki/Northern_Line_(Merseyrail)" class="mw-redirect" title="Northern Line (Merseyrail)">Northern Line</a> of the network, passengers must either use the Wirral Line and change at <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_Central_railway_station" title="Liverpool Central railway station">Liverpool Central station</a> or walk the short distance to the station.
</p>
